  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/persistence-agent.ts",
  "old_string": "  async getEntity(entityName: string, team: string): Promise<SharedMemoryEntity | null> {\n    try {\n      // Try GraphDB first\n      if (this.graphDB) {\n        // Use searchTerm for VKB API compatibility (namePattern not supported by VKB API)\n        const entities = await this.graphDB.queryEntities({\n          searchTerm: entityName,\n          team\n        });\n        // CRITICAL: Find exact match - searchTerm returns partial matches\n        // VKB API ignores namePattern and returns all entities without proper filtering\n        const exactMatch = entities?.find((e: any) =>\n          (e.name || e.entity_name) === entityName\n        );\n        if (exactMatch) {\n          return exactMatch as SharedMemoryEntity;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Fallback to shared memory\n      const sharedMemory = await this.loadSharedMemory();\n      return sharedMemory.entities.find(e => e.name === entityName) || null;",
  "new_string": "  async getEntity(entityName: string, team: string): Promise<SharedMemoryEntity | null> {\n    try {\n      // Try GraphDB first\n      if (this.graphDB) {\n        // Use searchTerm for VKB API compatibility (namePattern not supported by VKB API)\n        const entities = await this.graphDB.queryEntities({\n          searchTerm: entityName,\n          team\n        });\n\n        // DEBUG: Log what we received to diagnose the update vs create issue\n        log(`getEntity: searching for '${entityName}'`, 'debug', {\n          resultsCount: entities?.length || 0,\n          resultNames: entities?.slice(0, 5).map((e: any) => e.name || e.entity_name) || []\n        });\n\n        // CRITICAL: Find exact match - searchTerm returns partial matches\n        // VKB API ignores namePattern and returns all entities without proper filtering\n        const exactMatch = entities?.find((e: any) =>\n          (e.name || e.entity_name) === entityName\n        );\n        if (exactMatch) {\n          log(`getEntity: exact match found for '${entityName}'`, 'debug');\n          return exactMatch as SharedMemoryEntity;\n        }\n        log(`getEntity: no exact match for '${entityName}'`, 'debug');\n      }\n\n      // Fallback to shared memory\n      const sharedMemory = await this.loadSharedMemory();\n      const found = sharedMemory.entities.find(e => e.name === entityName) || null;\n      log(`getEntity: shared memory lookup for '${entityName}': ${found ? 'found' : 'not found'}`, 'debug');\n      return found;"
}

  "new_string": "  async getEntity(entityName: string, team: string): Promise<SharedMemoryEntity | null> {\n    try {\n      // Try GraphDB first\n      if (this.graphDB) {\n        // Use searchTerm for VKB API compatibility (namePattern not supported by VKB API)\n        const entities = await this.graphDB.queryEntities({\n          searchTerm: entityName,\n          team\n        });\n\n        // DEBUG: Log what we received to diagnose the update vs create issue\n        log(`getEntity: searching for '${entityName}'`, 'debug', {\n          resultsCount: entities?.length || 0,\n          resultNames: entities?.slice(0, 5).map((e: any) => e.name || e.entity_name) || []\n        });\n\n        // CRITICAL: Find exact match - searchTerm returns partial matches\n        // VKB API ignores namePattern and returns all entities without proper filtering\n        const exactMatch = entities?.find((e: any) =>\n          (e.name || e.entity_name) === entityName\n        );\n        if (exactMatch) {\n          log(`getEntity: exact match found for '${entityName}'`, 'debug');\n          return exactMatch as SharedMemoryEntity;\n        }\n        log(`getEntity: no exact match for '${entityName}'`, 'debug');\n      }\n\n      // Fallback to shared memory\n      const sharedMemory = await this.loadSharedMemory();\n      const found = sharedMemory.entities.find(e => e.name === entityName) || null;\n      log(`getEntity: shared memory lookup for '${entityName}': ${found ? 'found' : 'not found'}`, 'debug');\n      return found;"
}

'found' : 'not found'}`, 'debug');\n      return found;"

### Bash - 2025-12-26 19:48:13 UTC [20:48:13 CEST]

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree → nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "pwd",
  "description": "Confirm current project directory"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding
```

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree → nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{

}
